Citations for COVID-19 Related Violations
This list, updated
February 2023, details
2,096
COVID-19 related violations identified by Cal/OSHA.
Cal/OSHA only posts the violations after confirming the employer has received a copy of the citations.
Cal/OSHA posts a copy of the citation package with a hyperlink on the inspection number after ensuring
the documents comply with specified accessibility standards.
Limited information on the employerâs appeal of these citations is posted on the
federal OSHA.gov website
by searching with the Cal/OSHA inspection number. The chart includes the appeal date once
it has been scheduled by the
Occupational Safety and Health Appeals Board
and Cal/OSHA has been notified.

The Department of Industrial Relations (DIR) recognizes the importance of communicating effectively with individuals, including those with limited English proficiency. DIR is making an effort to provide 
    meaningful services for individuals that speak languages other than English.
If you need to access information in a language other than English:
Use the Google Translate function below:
Note:
This is a service provided by Google. Google Translate cannot translate all types of documents, and may not provide an exact translation.
Contact DIR to request an interpreter over the phone:
